security || This patch is a security patch (SRP). 

The patch fixes an integer overflow vulnerability in the rndis_wlan driver. By selecting a high value for "offset", an integer overflow could occur, bypassing the check for buffer overflow. This vulnerability could potentially be exploited by an attacker to execute arbitrary code or crash the system.

The patch modifies the code to use an unsigned integer for "len" and "offset" variables, preventing the possibility of integer overflow. It also adds additional checks to ensure that the length and offset values do not exceed the buffer size.

Overall, this patch addresses a security vulnerability and should be classified as a security patch (SRP).

security || This patch is a security patch (SRP). It fixes a potential livelock in the `return_unused_surplus_hugepages()` function in the `hugetlb` module. This fix prevents the potential livelock and improves the stability and reliability of the system.
